2b2(1): 'tshogs pa'i mchog/ mtshan dang dpe byad s+dzogs pa'i sku / rigs drug sems can kun gyi mgon/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i/ ston pa gnhen rab mi bo na/ dang po yae / 
2b3(1): sangs srid pa'i yul/ sems bskyed rnam bzhi'i 'od zer gyis/ tshad med thugs rje'i rang bzhin las/ ting 'dzin brgyad bcu'i ngng nyid ldan/ bar lha 'od gsal gnas nyid du / 
2b4(1): ye shes lha'i lung rgyud thob/ mgon btsun phya'i grong khyer du / ci snyed skal srid gtan la phabs/ 'og min dga' ldan grong khyer du / 'gro ba 'dul ba'i gshen rab la/

3a1(1): g.yo mnyam pa'i skur bzhugs nas/ 'gro ba'i don la tshad med kyi/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes grangs med spros/ mi thub brjid pa'i sku mchog la/ mtshan dang dpe / 
3a2(1): bya rab da +dzogs/ ma 'gags tshangs pa'i gsung dbyangs la/ brgyad bri bni stong bon ni 'byed/ mi 'byed mnyam pa'i thugs nyid la/ ce snyid gsal ba'i dgongs pa gsal
3a3(1): 'dod 'byung legs pa'i yon tan gsal/ gang la gang 'dul thabs su ston/ brtsal med lhun grub shrin las kyis/ 'gro ba'i don rnams mthar pbyin mdzad/ 'dul ba'i zhing 
3a4(1): khams phrag khrig spul/ ye shes sum brgya drug tu las/ yi gzhen sum brgya drug gur spros/ ting 'dzin yan lag brgyad bu las/ gsung drung don ldan brgyad gyur spul/ 
3a5(1): rnam mkhyen dbang po tshogs drug las/ rigs drug 'dul ba'i gnhen rab drug/ ha khrag rid dbugs rnam bzhi las/ 'byung ba'i bon po bzhe ru sprois/ sku ni 'gro ba'i dmigs 
3a6(1): yul du/ mthang snang tha dad so sor mdzes/ rang rang yid 'ong spro ba skyes/ gsung ni 'gro drug rna ba ru/ skad rigs mi mthun so sor go/ bden tshig nges pas phyogs bcur khyab/ 
3b1(1): thugs la sdzu 'prul bye ba brgya/ nyon mongs 'dod pas gdung ba sel/ nga dang zhugs kyis bde bar 'khod/ sems can dbang po'i spyod yul du/ ci 'dod nor bu rin po che/ thams 
3b2(1): cad phun sum tshogs par 'grub/ de'i tsho de' dus na/ ye nas bon nyid dbyings gnas su/ ya sangs sred pa'i thugs nyid la/ ci snyed dgongs pa dgu ru gsal/ 'khor ba dang ni 
3b3(1): myang 'das gnyis/ 'byed cing sud pa'i thabs rnams gsal/ sangs rgyas sems can dbye ba ru/ rtogs dang ma rtigs khyad par gsal/ dge dang las kyi bye brag la/ rgyu 'bras 
3b4(1): rnam par smin pa gsal/ bde ba dang ni sdug bsngal la/ dga' dang mi dga'i byung tsher gsal/ skyon dang yon tan thams cad la/ legs nyes so sor 'dzin par gsal/ mtho 
3b5(1): res ngan song gnas rnams la/ theg pa ging 'og khyad par 'phags/ rang rang gzhan gyi bye brag la/ ngdang bdag tu mthong ba gsal/ phye dang nang gi dbye ba ru/ snod dang bcud kyi bon 
3b6(1): rnams gsal/ thog mtha' dus kyi rang bzhin la/ snga phyir rnam grangs brtsis par gsal/ yul dang shes pa'i khyad par ru/ mtshan nyid rig cing gcod par gsal/ de ltar yi / 
4a1(1): srid thugs su g.yos/ dus dang srid pa'i skabs la yang / thabs dang shes rab zung 'brel te/ 'gro ba bkrid cing drang ba'i phyir/ mi g.so dbyings nas 'od pbyung zhing / tson 
4a2(1): nyid klong du brlabs bskyed nas/ s+dzu 'phrul mkha' las zer du spros/ yid las sprul pa'i khe' chung / shes rab rtsal ldan s+dzogs pa spul/ rig pa sdzu 'drul thabs ldan nas/ 
4a3(1): 'od kyi 'khor lo lnga la bcibs/ de dag snang med dbyings nas 'pyo/ bar lha 'od gsal gnas la byon/ skye mched mu bzhi'i gol sgrib 'geb/ srid pa yi sangs gnas su yang / 
4a4(1): gtsang ma rigs lnga'i shes sgrib sbyangs/ bsam gtan rigs bzhi'i zhing khams la/ ting 'dzin g.yo 'khrul mun pa sel/ dpag bsam ldzon pa'i rtse mo la/ brlab bdun 
4a5(1): khyung gi nya la bcabs/ yid ' rien chen khang bzang du/ lha rgyal dbang po brgya byin gyis/ yid bzhin nor bu'i thon lam prul/ rgyal chen rigs bzhi' gnas rnams la/ 
4a6(1): zhen chags mngon spyod sgrib pa bsal/ re rab bang rim khong seng na/ 'ga' 'da' slag can sprag rgyal gyis/ s+dzu 'drul rtsal gyi smon lam phrul/ ku ma ra tso' gdug / 
4b1(1): sems sul/ de nas re bdun rtse la byin/ g.yung drung khyim bdun gnas su yang / 'phel 'grib med pa'i smon lam btab/ gsu 'byug sngon po'i nya la bcibs/ mi yul 
4b2(1): gling bzhi 'khor ldeng nas/ snyan pa'i sgra skad kun tu grags/ gsal ba'i 'di ni phyogs bkur 'phros/ dus bzhi rgyal mos mdun bsdus nas/ sa g.yos re 'dar mtsho yang / 
4b3(1): 'tshol/ 'dzam gling 'ol mo lung rings su / gshen rab bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar byin/ bskor ba byed cing lha phyag 'tshal/ kun gyis dga' dang mchog tu skyes/ de la ston 
4b4(1): pas bka' stsal pa/ mtshan dang ldan pa'i khye' chung / mi mngon dbyings nas yas mar gshegs/ bar snang mkha' la sdzu 'dul bstan/ sa gzhi 'byung ba g.yo 'dar nas/ 
4b5(1): kun gyi dga' dang bskyed pa'i zhing / khyod dang po 'byungs gang zhig yin/ bar du bgrod lam ci lta bu/ tha ma grub pa ci ltar snyed/ de skad ston pas bka' stsal nas/ yid kyi 
4b6(1): khye'u chung zhus pa'i mdo/ ma sgrib thams cad rnam par gsal/ ci snyed mkhyen pa'i ston pa mchog/ bdag ni yid kyi khye'u chung / dang po byung ba'i khrungs nyid ni/ klong du rlabs 
5a1(1): bskyed dbyings nas g.yos/ mkha' las zer sros yid las spul/ sangs po 'brum khri' thugs kyi sras/ yi red nga du rang bzhin byang / s+dzu 'bhrul thabs la hun 
5a2(1): gyis grubbar du bgrod pa'i lam rnams ni/ dbyings su bgrod med 'od kyi lam/ ye shes rtse rgyal lnga ru gsal/ mkha' la hul med 'ja' tshen lam/ snang med tshe 
5a3(1): 'brul 'd du rgyu/ gzugs khams gnas 'grem bag sud sbyangs/ s+dzu 'drul mkha' lding rlabs kyi lam/ g.yo byed yid la yid kyi slabs/ sgra rgyal gsu 'byug rtsal gyi

5a5(1): srid pas grub/ thabs zhes 'du 'bral med pa grub/ de skad zhus nas thal mo sbyar/ de la ston pas bka' stsal pa/ bzhin bzang sgra mkhas blo gsal ba/ thabs ldan spyod

5b4(1): dpyad mdzod kyi sgrom nas pul/ ston pas 'gro ba'i don mdzad nas/ yon tan legs pa'i thabs rnams rgyas/ thabs dang shes rab zung du 'brel/ gto dpyad mdzod rnams 
5b5(1): seil bur 'byed/ gto bu la sogs sdig can yang / drangs nas thar pa'i dbyings su bstim/ dus de tsam na/ sred pa yid kyi khye' chung / ci snyed bsgrib med mkhyen pa gsal//
